data-pagefind-body="true" data-pagefind-meta="framework: react"><div class="overflow-hidden pb-8 pt-[calc(61px+2rem)] md:pt-8 md:max-w-3xl mx-auto prose dark:prose-invert dark:prose-code:bg-stone-900"><h1 id="installation-and-setup">Installation and Setup</h1>
<p>Add Jazz to your application in minutes. This setup covers standard front-end set up, and gives an overview of experimental SSR approaches.</p>
<p>Integrating Jazz with your existing app is straightforward. You&#x27;ll define data schemas that describe your application&#x27;s structure, then wrap your app with a provider that handles sync and storage. The whole process takes just three steps:</p>
<ol>
<li><a href="#install-dependencies">Install dependencies</a></li>
<li><a href="#write-your-schema">Write your schema</a></li>
<li><a href="#give-your-app-context">Give your app context</a></li>
</ol>
<p>Looking for complete examples? Check out our <a href="/examples">example applications</a> for chat apps, collaborative editors, and more.</p>
<h2 id="install-dependencies" class="group"><a href="#install-dependencies" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Install dependencies</span></h2>
<p>First, install the required packages:</p>
<div id="install-jazz" class="flex flex-col gap-4"><div class="flex gap-1 border-b border-stone-200 dark:border-stone-700"><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-transparent text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 hover:bg-stone-600/10 dark:hover:bg-white/10 active:bg-black/25 dark:active:bg-white/25 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-70 
                rounded-b-none border-b-2 transition-colors
                border-transparent hover:border-stone-300 dark:hover:border-stone-600
              " type="button">npm</button><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-transparent text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 hover:bg-stone-600/10 dark:hover:bg-white/10 active:bg-black/25 dark:active:bg-white/25 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-70 
                rounded-b-none border-b-2 transition-colors
                border-transparent hover:border-stone-300 dark:hover:border-stone-600
              " type="button">pnpm</button></div><div><div class="text-stone-500 dark:text-stone-400 p-4 text-center">No content available for tab: </div></div></div>
<h2 id="write-your-schema" class="group"><a href="#write-your-schema" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Write your schema</span></h2>
<p>Define your data schema using <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/overview">CoValues</a> from <code>jazz-tools</code>.</p>
<div class="flex items-center gap-2 font-bold"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-file-code h-4 w-4"><path d="M10 12.5 8 15l2 2.5"></path><path d="m14 12.5 2 2.5-2 2.5"></path><path d="M14 2v4a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h4"></path><path d="M15 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V7z"></path></svg> <!-- -->app/schema.ts</div>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  todos</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(TodoItem)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/overview">CoValues</a> for more information on how to define your schema.</p>
<h2 id="give-your-app-context" class="group"><a href="#give-your-app-context" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Give your app context</span></h2>
<p>Jazz depends on having context to know who&#x27;s reading and writing data.</p>
<p>You can make sure Jazz always has the right context by wrapping your application with a provider to connect to the Jazz network and define your data schema:</p>
<!-- -->

<!-- -->
<p>This setup handles:</p><ul>
<li>Connection to the Jazz sync server</li>
<li>Schema registration for type-safe data handling</li>
<li>Local storage configuration</li>
</ul><p>With this in place, you&#x27;re ready to start using Jazz hooks in your components. <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/subscription-and-loading#subscription-hooks">Learn how to access and update your data</a>.</p><h2 id="ssr-integration" class="group"><a href="#ssr-integration" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">SSR Integration</span></h2><p>Jazz&#x27;s default behaviour is to wait until the user&#x27;s account is loaded before rendering the provider&#x27;s children. This can be problematic on the server, where no account is available.</p><p>We can solve this by asking Jazz to render the children using an a read-only account that can be used without credentials, known as an &#x27;agent&#x27;.</p><p>Agents can access any data which is available to the public.</p><h3 id="enabling-provider-rendering-on-the-server" class="group"><a href="#enabling-provider-rendering-on-the-server" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Enabling Provider rendering on the server</span></h3><p>In order to tell Jazz to allow children to be loaded even in an account-less context, we can set the <code>enableSSR</code> setting on the provider.</p>
<div class="flex items-center gap-2 font-bold"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-file-code h-4 w-4"><path d="M10 12.5 8 15l2 2.5"></path><path d="m14 12.5 2 2.5-2 2.5"></path><path d="M14 2v4a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h4"></path><path d="M15 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V7z"></path></svg> <!-- -->app/components/JazzWrapper.tsx</div>

<h3 id="load-data-with-an-agent" class="group"><a href="#load-data-with-an-agent" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Load data with an agent</span></h3><p>In order to actually load and render data, you need to tell Jazz how to do this without an account. <p>Take a look at our <a href="https://github.com/garden-co/jazz/tree/main/examples/jazz-nextjs">Next.js example</a> to see a complete example of how to use SSR with Jazz.</p>
